This is a new fragrance. <b>Eros Energy</b> was launched in 2024. Top notes are Lemon, Blood Orange, Grapefruit, Lime, Sicilian Bergamot and Mandarin Orange; middle notes are Pink Pepper, White Amber and Black Currant; base notes are Oakmoss, Musk and Patchouli. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>Eros Energy is inspired by the breathtaking beauty of the Mediterranean coastline; the freshness of its scenery, the wildness of the air, and the luxury of a vast Italian vacation.</p>

<p>Channing Tatum stars in the Versace Eros campaign that debuts the collection’s latest eau de parfum pour homme, Eros Energy, and joins the existing Eros and Eros Flame fragrances.</p>

<p>Love, passion, desire and the breathtaking beauty of the Mediterranean shores form the inspirations of this olfactory creation. A unique freshness and sensuality to feel powerful, sexy and positive. Versace Eros Energy is the fragrance of a passionate man, master of himself and the codes of masculine allure.</p>

<p>Top notes: bergamot, blood orange, lime, mandarin, grapefruit, Lemon<br />
Heart notes: white amber, blackcurrant, pink pepper<br />
Base notes: patchouli, musk, oakmoss<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2324190" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jewmack"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1185045"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1185045.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jewmack" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Creed/Aventus-9828.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.9828.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Aventus"title="Aventus"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2324190ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2324190" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.87); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1185045">Jewmack</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-22"></span><fromunixtime unixtime="1729636344" class="vote-button-legend"></fromunixtime></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First thing I have to mention:<br />
I’m most definitely an Aventus Fanboy. It’s my most favorite fragrance of all time. <br />
With that being said; Blind bought this but at the same time… I didn’t. I read how many people mentioned how this smells like Aventus. So I kinda knew what was coming. <br />
<br />
I have plenty of Aventus type fragrances. CDNIM, Hacivat, two Aventus, Aventus cologne, explorer, etc. I’m sure I have more. <br />
<br />
Upon spraying my hand… yep! It smells like Aventus right off the jump. Which I am certainly not complaining about. But I can see this fragrance being played out by everybody. Since I’m certain more people buy Versace fragrances rather than Mont Blanc or CDNIM and etc. <br />
<br />
That being said, I do love it. I cannot dislike this scent profile. Although, if you have any of the Aventus type fragrances, there is no need to have this one. They ARE very similar off the rip. <br />
To me? It smells more like hacivat and CDNIM mixed. The dry down smells a lot more citrusy. But aventus aroma lingers. <br />
<br />
Should you buy it blind:<br />
<br />
Is 100 bucks too much for you?<br />
Are you tired of Aventus type scents?<br />
Are you gonna be angry when others wear it?<br />
No? Then, buy it. It smells amazing <br />
<br />
Would I have bought it if I smelled it beforehand? No, I wouldn’t have. The ONLY reason I would’ve bought it is to preserve the Aventus bottles. <br />
<br />
Good job versace</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2324190"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2324190#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2324058" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2321887" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Maya lilac"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1705079.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Maya lilac" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2321887ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2321887" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.77); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1705079">Maya lilac</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-20">10/20/24 10:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eros Energy is a true citrus bomb, in the best way possible. Versace launched it for some reason off season. This is one of those refreshing, invigorating, energetic types of spring and summer scent. Launched in the beginning of the fall….<br />
<br />
I’m aware that the entire Eros line is targeted towards men, but I love this! I was drawn in store to the bottle because of that gorgeous, vibrant, warm, rich medium yellow colour. It’s my favourite colour! But the juice is great. Opens very natural and realistic smelling, zesty, sparkling fresh, like you would sniff a smoothie made with all the citruses and some honey (syrupy sweetness coming from blackcurrants most likely). Very beautiful, bright and energising scent from the get go.<br />
<br />
Later on, as the scent develops on the blotter (I have only tried this on a blotter in store, so it’s a first impression) I can detect some woody nuances from moss and patchouli. Give it more balance and  more depth. It’s a very pleasant citrusy, fruity, fresh scent that I find totally unisex. It’s nothing groundbreaking as far as the scent goes, but it smells very natural, like fruits do when you cut them to eat them and make them a smoothie or a natural juice. Not the concentrated version from the store that smells very artificial and chemical! I find especially appealing here the combination of blood oranges, mandarin oranges and grapefruit in the opening. If you couldn’t guess by now, I am a citrus fan. <br />
<br />
I will revisit Eros Energy as soon as next spring approaches together with my husband. I might get a bottle for us to share..it’s not badly priced either for a 2024 release.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2321887"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2321887#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2321510" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Italian Bergamot + Mandarin Orange + Lime +  Grapefruit + White Tea + Woods + touch of vanilla + Pink Pepper + White Amber + Patchouli + Oakmoss + Musk + Sea Salt + Ambergris (Ambroxan)<br />
<br />
I've smelt this exact dna before!  This is a clone of Montblanc Explorer! (which is a clone of Aventus).  I feel Explorer is more unnerving acidic-sharp to the back of the nose, where Eros Energy has mellowed that note more evenly blended.<br />
<br />
It's actually really good!!<br />
Versace actually has a hit here, even though this is an exact clone of another fragrance, but will be a big seller because Versace has billions of dollars of marketing and shelf space contracts behind it.<br />
Mass appealing, summer high heat, dumb reach fragrance.<br />
Woman LOVE this dna, so much some genres of women wear it.  And with that, this is absolutely gender-neutral. <br />
Lasted 24 hours on my skin! :S<br />
<br />
Scent Quality: Aventus ($$$) &gt; Eros Energy ($$) &gt; Explorer ($)<br />
<br />
3.5/5 Woofs!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2321510"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2321510#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2320928" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2319636" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EauDeSparta"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2290486.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EauDeSparta" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2319636ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2319636" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2290486">EauDeSparta</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 06:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I had the opportunity to try Eros Energy at a Sephora store. It's a completely citrus-themed summer fragrance, which could be quite weak in terms of longevity and projection during the winter months. At first sniff, I can say it smells just like lemon. As time goes on, the scent developed a sweeter character on my skin and resembles Creed Aventus. If you're looking for a unique fragrance, it might be more beneficial to invest in different alternatives. Lastly, while the bottle retains the lines of the original Eros bottle, I must say I'm not fond of the yellow color. 6.5/10.<br />
<br />
Eros Energy'yi Sephora mağazasında deneme fırsatı buldum. Tamamen citrus temalı, yazlık bir parfüm; kış aylarında kalıcılık ve yayılım açısından oldukça zayıf kalabilecek düzeyde. Açılışta, ilk kokladığınızda sadece limon gibi koktuğunu söyleyebilirim. Zaman ilerledikçe koku, tenimde daha tatlı bir karaktere büründü ve Creed Aventus'a benzer bir kokuya sahip olduğunu düşünüyorum. Eğer özgün bir koku arıyorsanız, farklı alternatiflere yönelmek daha faydalı olabilir. Son olarak, şişesi orijinal Eros şişesinin hatlarını korusa da, sarı rengin pek hoşuma gitmediğini belirtmeliyim. 6.5/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2319636"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2319636#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319019" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I ended up buying it for the full retail price and I’m so happy. I definitely think it’s worth it, I love simple citrus fragrances and this does that so well.<br />
<br />
10/10.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2319019"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2319019#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2318527" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Honestly, I was expecting something bold and irresistible, but instead, I got smacked in the face with the scent of freshly squeezed lemon juice. It’s like I’m wearing a citrus cleaner instead of a cologne. Who knew smelling like a kitchen counter was a vibe? If you’re into smelling like you just finished scrubbing down your countertops with a lemon wedge, this one's for you. As for me, I’ll stick to fragrances that don't make me feel like I should be mopping the floor.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2316005"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2316005#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2314827" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I thought this was stupid at first. "It's just some lemon"<br />
I got over that.<br />
<br />
This is very straight forward...the marketing, the target season, everything. Yes it was dumb for them to release it AFTER the summer in the US<br />
<br />
But really, after testing this a few times I love it. <br />
If you smell deeper you can sense the different citruses. <br />
This is basically like aventus cologne, but with a little more realistic lemon and at a 3rd of the price.<br />
<br />
There are no good clones of aventus cologne on the market. So for this to be about equal quality and 80% the scent profile, it's absolutely worth my money, and I will be picking up a bottle of this at some point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1552217">AnosmiaAnosognosia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-13">10/13/24 12:46</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I see a few comments saying things like "NOTHING LIKE AVENTUS" or "people who say this smells like Aventus, don't own Aventus" is so bizarre to me. No one is saying it is a one to one clone, but it's clearly in that ballpark. Even if you don't own Aventus and have a clone, you can easily draw a comparison. It is in that "style" or "DNA".<br />
<br />
I happen to love Energy and will buy it when it is found with regularity on discounters. The fragrance collection I have displayed on here is accurate as it can be. I do have couple that aren't on this site yet. I own a couple of bottles of Aventus and Absolu and have tested Cologne plenty to know I didn't want to spend Creed money on a weaker version of the original, but Cologne smells great too. <br />
<br />
Eros Energy: Citrus bomb, check. Light birchy-woodiness in the drydown, check. For the newer less enthusiastic fragrance consumers, this would be a great introduction to this style of fragrance. For the snobs, not so much. If mega-citrus is not your thing, stay far away from this. Because this one is so easy to find and test, figure it out for yourself. I think it lives up to what the name suggests. Energetic, zingy-zesty, bright fragrance. One thing that rings true as well, is that it does not smell like any of the Eros line.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2314583"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2314583#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2314089" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Wait for discounters. I paid retail with a wicked promo but I wouldnt have otherwise. Its commendable but not something I couldnt wait to buy. I liked the top and mid on the card better than on skin, but I enjoy the drydown overall on both card and skin and am happy with the purchase overall. Lasting power is average, projection is good. Grinded lemon zest sprinkled with freshly squeezed lemon juice!<br />
Most of lemon scents smell like cleaning products, but this one smells so fresh and natural, I love it so much!<br />
<br />
That lemon explosion last for about half an hour, after that it starts to fade away (but not completely) so you notice some amber, mossy and slightly woody/sweet notes but it never gets heavy, it's warm but still fresh.<br />
<br />
It's not super strong, which I like because you won't suffocate everyone around you, but you'll feel it on your skin for hours.<br />
<br />
If you're a fan of previous Eros fragrances - keep in mind that this is something completely different.<br />
I always found other Eros products too heavy and kinda headache inducing, so I went to smell this thinking "let's see how bad this one can be" and I was so pleasantly surprised!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
Like yes, this isn’t super original or overly interesting, the release was a disaster with delays and whatnot, but with all that aside, I think this is generally a pretty good cologne. It’s zingy, bright and a bit sweet. <br />
<br />
I’ll be honest, you shouldn’t buy this YET considering most retailers are pricing this at $150-160 for 100ml. It’s hitting discounters soon starting at $115CAD for 100ml which is already a solid price for a new release. If you wait like 6-12 additional months it’ll probably be just south of what Eros Flame costs.<br />
<br />
I know a lot of the negative ratings so far have to do with review bombers and kids who heard their favourite fragrance influencer bash this for “smelling like aventus,” it doesn’t. I wanna bet a lot of the people leaving bad reviews haven’t even smelt this yet considering it just now made it to retailers.<br />
<br />
7/10 as of October 2024, I’ll probably pick this up in Q2 2025 once the price has dropped considerably.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2310743"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2310743#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2309343" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2307917" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="realmarkvon"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1171333"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1171333.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="realmarkvon" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2307917ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2307917" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1171333">realmarkvon</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-07">10/07/24 11:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is a much better version of Mont Blanc Explorer. <br />
<br />
As everyone has said, this opens up with a super blast of bergamot and lime. There are other citruses too, but these are the main players.<br />
<br />
After a few minutes you can start to smell the base notes emerge. Whereas Mont Blanc Explorer base came off unpleasant and jarring (I gave it away), this Energy's base continues to smell good. I still smell this on my skin after 18 hours.<br />
<br />
For the money, just get Insurrection Pure II.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2307917"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2307917#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2307728" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This scent also has the best longevity out of all exclusively citrus fragrances I have tested so far.<br />
Definitely a spring-summer day fragrance.<br />
I personally like this and would wear this!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2303994"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2303994#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2303724" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I love the color of the bottle and cap, but…<br />
The cologne is very citrus heavy in the opening. I love citrus, but my wife thought it was too much. The opening last for about 3 hours, which is a long time for a citrus opening (I love lemon). She thought the drydown was nice, but not as good as some of my other colognes. The drydown has that soft wood and smokiness in it. It doesn’t project like when you first sprayed it, but it’ll be smelled when you pass by others.<br />
<br />
If you want an example for the opening, think of Aventus Cologne, but much more rugged lemon and orange oil in it. It does have a very slight smokiness in the background.<br />
<br />
If you want to buy for yourself, then go for it. It smells great, but if you want to attract somebody near you, then maybe go with something else.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2302473"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2302473#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2302309" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1067640">seldomseen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-01">10/01/24 16:11</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>As others have already indicated, minus the pineapple note, Eros Energy smells similar to Aventus and many of it's clones such as PV/PVI/CDNIM/Explorer/et cetera, especially when it reaches the dry down stage. However, don't be fooled by the citrusy opening, which actually last quite a few hours. 😊 Because Energy actually feels and wears like a dark/heavy/birchy masculine batch of Aventus with citrus notes, opposed to pineapple. <br />
<br />
Consequently, if you actually own and have given Energy a full days wearing, you will understand why it was incorporated into the Eros line. As Energy's potent base notes of Oakmoss, Musk and Patchouli notes makes it feel like a resinous/citrusy/fragrant winter fragrance, and not a traditional citrusy summer fragrance. The citrus notes simply help to soften and sweeten the base notes and make the fragrance pop and sparkle when you wear it. 🥳 <br />
<br />
Eros Energy is a solid release and worth a full-bottle purchase especially if discounted 15% or more off retail. Performance is almost nuclear too. Most people will yield 24hrs, unless you have pig's skin! 😖🤣😂😃 Energy is an excellent winter fragrance, especially if you want something masculine and different from all the cheap syrupy sweet fall/winter fragrances flooding the market! I suspect Energy will overwhelm mofos that wear it in hot weather and may interpret the base notes as body odor. 💯<br />
<br />
Overall: 8.75/10 - Only because the Aventus DNA is a bit played out now.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2301685"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2301685#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2300184" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2298359" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Jaime N"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1818218"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1818218.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Jaime N" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Chanel/Egoiste-Platinum-614.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.614.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Egoiste Platinum"title="Egoiste Platinum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2298359ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2298359" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.8); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1818218">Jaime N</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-28">09/28/24 17:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This smells like Lemon Calippo. Pure and simple. And it's great. Yes, it's synthetic, it's a synthetic citrus bomb, but it's good. A very brisk, full, fresh, slightly sweet citrus bomb. At 41, I'm a little past the age where I reach for fragrances like the ones in the Eros family. Not that there's anything wrong with that. And that won't surely stop me from acknowledging that this should be a hit of a fragrance, especially among the crowd under 30. <br />
The citrus elements remain very present and dominant throughout the very long and seemingly linear drydown, but after an hour or so the oakmoss begins to add a very interesting woody earthy element that pushes this to a slightly more mature level. I guess that's where the association with Aventus comes from, as I don't see any other similarities during the very lively and vibrant citric first couple of hours. The added bonus: the performance on this thing is just fantastic - I did a spray on the back of my hand more than 9 hours ago and it's still VERY noticeable in the air as I write this (funnily enough, didn't last much on paper strip. Go figure). I can't think of a longer lasting, better performing true fresh fragrance in the designer realm right now. Stunning!<br />
<br />
I only wish I was 20 again...<br />
<br />
7.5/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2298359"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2298359#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2298251" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2297632" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="mdnial"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2072181"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="mdnial" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2297632ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2297632" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2072181">mdnial</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-28">09/28/24 02:34</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The OG Eros and Flame are quite unique. This new version of Eros is nothing but an impression of Aventus</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2297632"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2297632#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2297582" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2297582" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="TheDogfatherHTX"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1824841.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="TheDogfatherHTX" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/The-Woods-Collection/Dusk-63711.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.63711.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Dusk"title="Dusk"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2297582ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2297582" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1824841">TheDogfatherHTX</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-28">09/28/24 01:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The newest entry into Versace's Eros line; Eros Energy. I knew from the moment I tried this off a tester strip at Macy's that I would have to get it. As soon as it came up for sale on discounter websites I scooped it up to complete my Eros collection. I've tried and tested all the scents in the Eros line, and I've loved all of them. Will Energy make it 5 for 5? Let's get into it;<br />
<br />
Scent:<br />
Opening is citrusy, juicy, and bright. The primary notes I get are lemon, lime, blood orange, and grapefruit. The strongest of the notes are the lemon and lime. Both notes are sharp, juicy, and ride the line between realistic and synthetic. This is followed by the blood orange and grapefruit. The blood orange doubles down on the orange-focused citrus and adds a healthy dose of sweetness, while the grapefruit adds a hint of bitter rindy-ness. There's also a creaminess to the opening. I'm not sure where it comes from, but it's definitely noticeable to me and gives the opening a "yellow starburst candy" accord to my nose. I think it's absolutely delicious smelling and gives the opening a "citrus gourmand" edge. The dry down is citrusy, woody, and fresh. The primary notes I get are lemon, oak moss, blood orange, and black currant. The strongest of the notes are the lemon and oak moss. The lemon still has the same tart and juicy accord from the opening, while the oak moss has accompanied it for a dose of its signature inky woodiness. This is followed by the blood orange and black currant. The blood orange still carries the sweet citrus notes from the opening, and the black currant rounds out the dry down with its signature tangy, green, and slightly ammoniac accord. I know what you're thinking, "Black currant? So it smells like Creed Aventus?". In answer to that question; yes but not entirely. The dry down does certainly give me Aventus vibes with the lemon, black currant, and oak moss; so parallels could definitely be drawn between the two. One could almost be fooled into believing this is an Aventus inspired fragrance. But Energy is overall much fresher and citrus forward, and also lacks the smokiness of Aventus. In fact, I would say it matches Aventus Cologne more so than OG Aventus. Overall the scent profile of Energy is incredible; the opening is my favorite part but the dry down is equally enjoyable.<br />
<br />
Performance:<br />
Initial projection is strong at around 6 feet. Sillage is enormous with an unmistakeable scent trail. After a few hours the projection and sillage were unchanged, still very strong. At the 7 hour mark the projection was right outside arms length and the scent trail was still noticeable. At around the 10 hour mark the projection was gone but there was still a light scent trail being left. The fragrance became a skin scent shortly thereafter.<br />
<br />
When to wear:<br />
Versace was pretty late to the party waiting until September to release this, because this is a Spring/Summer fragrance through and through. Eros Energy is suited most for daytime and is very easy wearing. While the opening tailor-made for being out in the sun, the dry down gives this fragrance enough versatility to work at the office or on dates as well, just be careful not to overspray.<br />
<br />
Blind buy:<br />
If you like heavy-handed citrus fragrances, or you like the Aventus-style DNA, this is a safe blind buy for you.<br />
<br />
Final verdict:<br />
This fragrance has everything most people are looking for in a fragrance; a mass-appealing scent, powerful performance, versatility, and that compliment factor. Unfortunately fragrance snobs are probably going to hate on this because it's Versace and it's not "interesting" enough for their palette, and I can understand that. It's not breaking any molds and it shares strong similarities with the Aventus/Aventus Cologne DNA. But here's the fact of the matter; not every fragrance has to be a deep dive into high art perfumery. The Eros line is one of the best selling men's fragrance lines for a reason, it smells great and gets positive attention. Eros Energy is no exception. Sometimes it's okay to appreciate a fragrance for what it is without trying to compare it to something 3 or 4 times it's price point. This will be joining the rest of the Eros line on my "love it" shelf, and I'm not ashamed to say that. Are you?<br />
<br />
Scent: 10/10<br />
Longevity: 8/10<br />
Sillage: 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2297582"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2297582#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2297427" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2296265" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="chrisivE"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2191906"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="chrisivE" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gucci/Gucci-Guilty-Absolute-43040.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.43040.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gucci Guilty Absolute"title="Gucci Guilty Absolute"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2296265ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2296265" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2191906">chrisivE</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 17:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eros Energy by Versace begins with an intense citrus medley, dominated by a sharp lemon note that brings a limoncello-like freshness. This lemon note is the star for the first 20 minutes, but as it starts to mellow, other citrus elements like lime, orange, and mandarin emerge, each contributing its own unique twist. The lime adds a slightly sour, tangy aspect, reminiscent of a cocktail like a Moscow Mule, while the orange and mandarin infuse a subtle sweetness. Together, they create a vibrant, zesty opening that captures the essence of a summer day.<br />
<br />
As the fragrance develops, the heart and base notes begin to add complexity and depth. Pink pepper introduces a hint of spice, providing a warm contrast to the citrus brightness. The white amber contributes a creamy, slightly sweet undertone that balances the sharpness of the citrus, giving the fragrance a smooth, velvety texture. While the black currant isn't distinctly prominent, it likely plays a role in bridging the fruity top notes with the deeper, more grounded base. This transition is seamless, preventing the fragrance from becoming overly sharp or one-dimensional.<br />
<br />
In the dry down, the fragrance settles into a harmonious blend where musk and oakmoss come to the forefront, adding a fresh yet earthy finish. The musk enhances the citrus' freshness, while the oakmoss lends a subtle, natural earthiness that lingers on the skin. Patchouli adds a final touch of sweetness and depth. They all rounding out the composition and making it more than just a simple citrus scent. The result is a refreshing, sophisticated fragrance that's perfect for hot summer days, offering both the invigorating zest of citrus and the comforting warmth of earthy, spicy notes.<br />
<br />
<b> In short: Eros Energy starts with a burst of bright citrus, evolves with spicy and creamy nuances, and finishes with a fresh, earthy base, making it an ideal summer fragrance with a blend of both vibrancy and depth. </b></p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2295772" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Fortyfree"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1631067"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1631067.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Fortyfree" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2295772ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2295772" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1631067">Fortyfree</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 09:26</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Opens with a light, sweet pineapple note, it's a little floral, sparkling, and with a touch of something aquatic. <br />
Has a citrus lemon backbone, fruity notes, and smells clean overall. There's a little spice too, and a metallic musk develops after an hour. It's airy and expansive, gets a little sour after 3hrs. <br />
Starts to become aromatic after a while on the skin, leans a bit green, has the well known Creed musk accord (which puts the wearer in mind of mountain air.) Has more spice &amp; conifer wood notes, before turning to a lemon aroma again.<br />
<br />
Performance was good on me, great projection and lasted on the back of my arm until the following morning. It's a persistent smell that does run the risk of becoming boring, even though it's very pleasant. <br />
<br />
Best for guys, spring and summertime. <br />
<br />
It did remind me of Aventus, minus the smoky-chypre facets. It feels to me as if Versace realised how popular the pineapple Aventus DNA is, and felt they couldn't afford not to have their own take on it?</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; That being said, it is very lemony for the first hour or so then calms down nicely and lets the other notes shine. The opening reminds me a bit of the opening of Y Eau Fraiche then it fades into an Aventus-y scent minus the smokiness. I would never guess this was an Eros as I don't get any of that DNA at all. Not a bad scent at all but if you already have CDNIM this might be redundant unless you just want something that's ever so slightly fresher.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1722305">ThatBlindbuyGuy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-16">09/16/24 17:35</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Eros Energy opens with a fizzy burst of citrus, reminiscent of a juicy mix of lime, lemon, and orange. It offers a lively, refreshing start very similar to Aaron Terence Hughes’ Supernova but lacks the salty ambergris found in Supernova. The dry down is simpler yet nuanced, featuring a touch of oakmoss, pink pepper, and patchouli, alongside a generous amount of white amber. This white amber reminds me of a mix of clean musks, sandalwood, and white woods, resulting in a smooth, refined finish with a clean woody profile. I don’t understand the comparison between Eros Energy and Creed Aventus though, as Aventus is well known for its peppery and leathery notes and smoky birch, which are quite different from Eros Energy’s very citrus-heavy and clean woody profile.<br />
<br />
As I mentioned in my first impressions review, Eros Energy is very, very similar to ATH's Supernova. If you already own Supernova, you might not need this one, and vice versa.<br />
<br />
Overall score: 8.5/10 , the opening is beautifully juicy and effervescent, while the dry down presents a very simple, clean woody scent—perfect for warm or even hot sunny days</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It’s basically CDNI without the smoke. If you have CDNI and want a day time cologne then this is it. Compared to Mont Blanc Explorer, it’s basically that plus a ton of condensed citrus. I would get this over Explorer and CDNI but probably not over Aventus Cologne. However, I would probably need to test this with Aventus Cologne to get a better idea of which one I like better. This smells like those lemon head candies or any other type of lemon candy for about 5 minutes and then immediately you get the Creed Aventus/Montblanc Explorer/Club de Nuit dry down, but in my opinion it doesn't smell as high quality as either of those. I love Versace but this is a disappointment. A major let down.<br />
<br />
Edit: This has a more smoothed out dry down. A semi-sweet, semi-creamy dry down. Not really vanillic, but you get a tad bit of fruitiness with a little bit of a lotion/soapy scent. Still not worth it because by the time it gets to this point in the dry-down you can't even smell it anymore; I have to sniff my hand where I sprayed it in order to smell this and it's only been about 5 hours. Weak projection, minimal sillage. Lemonhead opening, Aventus mid, semi fruity creamy dry down that is undetectable. <br />
5/10 for me. If this eventually gets discounted to like $40-$50 then maybe it'll be worth it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2281462"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2281462#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2281330" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; And since there is so much Aventus talk around this, I sprayed Mont Blanc Explorer on the other arm. <br />
Off the top, lots of citrus, bright and zesty. Then there is some herbaceous/green notes that come out in the mid. So far, so good. It’s the dry down …like 1-2 hours later where the Aventus vibe shows itself. Compared to the MBE…if that is a half brother to Aventus, VEE is a 2nd cousin. It doesn’t get as close as MBE, but the familiarity is there. I’ve never smelled Aventus Cologne, so maybe there is a closer similarity to that? padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2251297">Chinspike</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-11">09/11/24 23:28</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This smells awesome to me.  Absolute lemon bomb opening, but in the best possible way.  It's so good, I couldn't stop smelling my arm.  In the drydown I don't know how it's supposed to be an aventus clone because it still smells like lemon, just much less intense with some woody and amber notes to round it out.<br />
<br />
I'm kind of glad it doesn't have the vanilla of eros, and I say this as someone who loves vanilla, as I think it would dilute the freshness.  It is a bit weird to call it an eros flanker when it doesn't have much at all in common with eros or flame though.  If you ignore the name and just enjoy it for what it is, which is delicious lemons, it's great.<br />
<br />
Sillage seems lower than flame and it faded to a skin scent after about 6 hours, but it stayed on my skin until I showered. That said, definitely possible it was projecting longer but I just stopped noticing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2279887"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2279887#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279526" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's closer to Dior Homme Cologne and Jimmy Choo Man Ice in my opinion.<br />
<br />
So I think everyone can agree that this is a citrus bomb; absolutely spectacular combination but it's the lemon that stands out. And it dries down to a clean musk.<br />
<br />
I've never tried Aventus so can't compare but I have owned Explorer and this is better; but again they are similar.<br />
<br />
Longevity is excellent and a good compliment getter. But in reality if you have any of the comparative fragrances mentioned above this will be redundant.<br />

But that said, it is excellent and what I like.<br />
<br />
8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2279526"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2279526#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279511" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1360486">Steven221283</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-11">09/11/24 07:12</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The opening is really nice and attention grabbing - a citrus explosion. As it dries down it basically starts to become an Aventus clone, which isn't necessarily a bad thing, it's a tried and tested DNA that most people like (I'd recommend Aaron Terence Hughes Supernova if you want the best thing in this ballpark, though). After about 3-4 hours it has dried  to a pretty generic, woody fragrance with a hint of citrus still there - it doesn't really smell like Aventus anymore at this point, it's more in the vain of the likes of DHS 2021 at this point. A decent enough release, but has no right to have the Eros name as there are zero similarities, and the only standout part is the short lived opening - though the rest is nice. I think it will have plenty of fans.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2279044"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2279044#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2278858" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; This is a lemon bomb, that's it, that's all this fragrance is. It smells like a good cheapy, not like some high end male fragrance, what Aventus is.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2278086"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2278086#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2277914" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; If anything, this looks way more like Flame, but a "more bright and juicy" version. And flame was alright.<br />
<br />
It straight-up reminds me of those soluble grapefruit water syrup drinks you get after football practice as a kid. It's just musky citrus from start to finish.<br />
<br />
Regurgitated echo chamber vomit talk. I'm starting to think many people in this community just watch fragrance YouTube/TikTok all day and click Amazon affiliate links. "Oh no, they're copying the greatest frag of all time again!" Can we stop the BS already? There exists more than your 3-mosquito spray fragrance rotation of Club de Nuit and whatever. Get out of the parrot box and think for yourself!<br />
<br />
EDIT: Upon further investigation, I finally know what this smells like! CLEARLY, it is Dora the Explorer from Dora and Boots. Sorry, guys, I wish I picked up on it sooner!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2275249"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2275249#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2275222" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2041177">renomen43</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-06">09/06/24 18:29</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Had a chance today to try this in the store.<br />
2 sprays on a paper strip and it instantly hit me what it reminded me of: Supremacy Not Only Intense by Afnan.<br />
<br />
No, they are not exactly the same. The citruses are not that sharp and heavy in Eros Energy and it dries down to a less mossy, more musky and ambery base than SNOI. However they smell extremely similar for the first 1-2 hours, just like any Aventus inspired fragrance. Whoever says it doesn't have the characteristics of Aventus clones is lying big time or doesn't know what he's talking about. After that 1-2 hour period the differences show clearly.<br />
<br />
Despite SNOI being unpleasant for my nose in the first 30 minutes, I’d still buy that over Eros Energy. Mainly because of the price but also because Energy is a lighter scent overall.<br />
<br />
I didn’t expect this scent profile at all, I mean I knew it was a citrus-heavy fragrance but let’s just say it’s a strange flanker nonethless.<br />
<br />
SNOI costs €43 while Energy sits around €73 where I live. If you own anything with the legendary Aventus DNA, don’t buy this fragrance. You don’t need it then.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2274099"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2274099#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2273776" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I guarantee you the people over at Versace could care less...Doesn't effect them in the slightest. Some of us actually want to learn and know about new releases and legitimately what others have to say.<br />
<br />
As for my opinion on Versace Eros Energy?  It's a lemony Aventus Cologne style fragrance, as others have stated.  Lasts a good 6hrs or so on my skin and projects at an arms length for the majority of time...If that is your vibe, go for it!  May have some redundancy if you own Aventus, CDNI or Explorer, but i enjoy it...Will eventually be a cheapie gem once it shows up at rack stores and online discounters.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; It smells like a nice citrus fuzzy shower gel. Very easy to wear, super versatile, office friendly, not too loud either. <br />
The projection is comparable to Eros EDP and Eros Flame but it doesn’t smell anything like those 2 ! But it shares more similarities with Eros flame than the original but it isn’t redundant to own both that’s for sure. <br />
<br />
88 euros for 100ml. <br />
<br />
A very good pickup for an all year scent !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="92647"comment_id="2255246"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Eros-Energy-92647.html?ccid=2255246#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2265269" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
